## Schemas

### ApiextensionsCrossplaneIoV1alpha1CompositionSpec

CompositionSpec specifies the desired state of the definition.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**from** `required`|[ApiextensionsCrossplaneIoV1alpha1CompositionSpecFrom](#apiextensionscrossplaneiov1alpha1compositionspecfrom)|from||
|**reclaimPolicy**|"Retain" | "Delete"|ReclaimPolicy specifies what will happen to composite resource dynamically provisioned using this composition when their namespaced referrer is deleted. The "Delete" policy causes the composite resource to be deleted when its namespaced referrer is deleted. The "Retain" policy causes the composite resource to be retained, in binding phase "Released", when its namespaced referrer is deleted. The "Retain" policy is used when no policy is specified, however the "Delete" policy is set at dynamic provisioning time if no policy is set.||
|**to** `required`|[[ApiextensionsCrossplaneIoV1alpha1CompositionSpecToItems0](#apiextensionscrossplaneiov1alpha1compositionspectoitems0)]|To is the list of target resources that make up the composition.||
|**writeConnectionSecretsToNamespace** `required`|str|WriteConnectionSecretsToNamespace specifies the namespace in which the connection secrets of composite resource dynamically provisioned using this composition will be created.||

### CacheCrossplaneIoV1alpha1RedisClusterSpecClassRef

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**apiVersion**|str|API version of the referent.||
|**fieldPath**|str|If referring to a piece of an object instead of an entire object, this string should contain a valid JSON/Go field access statement, such as desiredState.manifest.containers[2]. For example, if the object reference is to a container within a pod, this would take on a value like: "spec.containers{name}" (where "name" refers to the name of the container that triggered the event) or if no container name is specified "spec.containers[2]" (container with index 2 in this pod). This syntax is chosen only to have some well-defined way of referencing a part of an object. TODO: this design is not final and this field is subject to change in the future.||
|**kind**|str|Kind of the referent. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#types-kinds||

|**namespace**|str|Namespace of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/namespaces/||
|**resourceVersion**|str|Specific resourceVersion to which this reference is made, if any. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#concurrency-control-and-consistency||
|**uid**|str|UID of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#uids||
### CacheCrossplaneIoV1alpha1RedisClusterSpecClassSelector

A ClassSelector specifies labels that will be used to select a resource class for this claim. If multiple classes match the labels one will be chosen at random.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**matchExpressions**|[[CacheCrossplaneIoV1alpha1RedisClusterSpecClassSelectorMatchExpressionsItems0](#cachecrossplaneiov1alpha1redisclusterspecclassselectormatchexpressionsitems0)]|matchExpressions is a list of label selector requirements. The requirements are ANDed.||
|**matchLabels**|{str:str}|matchLabels is a map of {key,value} pairs. A single {key,value} in the matchLabels map is equivalent to an element of matchExpressions, whose key field is "key", the operator is "In", and the values array contains only "value". The requirements are ANDed.||
### CacheCrossplaneIoV1alpha1RedisClusterSpecClassSelectorMatchExpressionsItems0

A label selector requirement is a selector that contains values, a key, and an operator that relates the key and values.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**key** `required`|str|key is the label key that the selector applies to.||
|**operator** `required`|str|operator represents a key's relationship to a set of values. Valid operators are In, NotIn, Exists and DoesNotExist.||
|**values**|[str]|values is an array of string values. If the operator is In or NotIn, the values array must be non-empty. If the operator is Exists or DoesNotExist, the values array must be empty. This array is replaced during a strategic merge patch.||

| name | type | description | default value |

|**matchExpressions**|[[ComputeCrossplaneIoV1alpha1KubernetesClusterSpecClassSelectorMatchExpressionsItems0](#computecrossplaneiov1alpha1kubernetesclusterspecclassselectormatchexpressionsitems0)]|matchExpressions is a list of label selector requirements. The requirements are ANDed.||
|**matchLabels**|{str:str}|matchLabels is a map of {key,value} pairs. A single {key,value} in the matchLabels map is equivalent to an element of matchExpressions, whose key field is "key", the operator is "In", and the values array contains only "value". The requirements are ANDed.||
### ComputeCrossplaneIoV1alpha1KubernetesClusterSpecClassSelectorMatchExpressionsItems0

A label selector requirement is a selector that contains values, a key, and an operator that relates the key and values.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**key** `required`|str|key is the label key that the selector applies to.||
|**operator** `required`|str|operator represents a key's relationship to a set of values. Valid operators are In, NotIn, Exists and DoesNotExist.||
|**values**|[str]|values is an array of string values. If the operator is In or NotIn, the values array must be non-empty. If the operator is Exists or DoesNotExist, the values array must be empty. This array is replaced during a strategic merge patch.||
### ComputeCrossplaneIoV1alpha1KubernetesClusterSpecResourceRef

A ResourceReference specifies an existing managed resource, in any namespace, to which this resource claim should attempt to bind. Omit the resource reference to enable dynamic provisioning using a resource class; the resource reference will be automatically populated by Crossplane.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**apiVersion**|str|API version of the referent.||
|**fieldPath**|str|If referring to a piece of an object instead of an entire object, this string should contain a valid JSON/Go field access statement, such as desiredState.manifest.containers[2]. For example, if the object reference is to a container within a pod, this would take on a value like: "spec.containers{name}" (where "name" refers to the name of the container that triggered the event) or if no container name is specified "spec.containers[2]" (container with index 2 in this pod). This syntax is chosen only to have some well-defined way of referencing a part of an object. TODO: this design is not final and this field is subject to change in the future.||
|**kind**|str|Kind of the referent. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#types-kinds||
|**name**|str|Name of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#names||
|**namespace**|str|Namespace of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/namespaces/||
|**resourceVersion**|str|Specific resourceVersion to which this reference is made, if any. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#concurrency-control-and-consistency||
|**uid**|str|UID of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#uids||
### ComputeCrossplaneIoV1alpha1KubernetesClusterSpecWriteConnectionSecretToRef

|**engineVersion**|"9.6" | "11"|EngineVersion specifies the desired PostgreSQL engine version. Allowed Versions: 9.6 and 11.||
|**resourceRef**|[DatabaseCrossplaneIoV1alpha1PostgreSQLInstanceSpecResourceRef](#databasecrossplaneiov1alpha1postgresqlinstancespecresourceref)|resource ref||

### DatabaseCrossplaneIoV1alpha1PostgreSQLInstanceSpecClassRef

A ClassReference specifies a resource class that will be used to dynamically provision a managed resource when the resource claim is created.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**apiVersion**|str|API version of the referent.||
|**fieldPath**|str|If referring to a piece of an object instead of an entire object, this string should contain a valid JSON/Go field access statement, such as desiredState.manifest.containers[2]. For example, if the object reference is to a container within a pod, this would take on a value like: "spec.containers{name}" (where "name" refers to the name of the container that triggered the event) or if no container name is specified "spec.containers[2]" (container with index 2 in this pod). This syntax is chosen only to have some well-defined way of referencing a part of an object. TODO: this design is not final and this field is subject to change in the future.||
|**kind**|str|Kind of the referent. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#types-kinds||
|**name**|str|Name of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#names||
|**namespace**|str|Namespace of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/namespaces/||
|**resourceVersion**|str|Specific resourceVersion to which this reference is made, if any. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#concurrency-control-and-consistency||
|**uid**|str|UID of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#uids||
### DatabaseCrossplaneIoV1alpha1PostgreSQLInstanceSpecClassSelector

A ClassSelector specifies labels that will be used to select a resource class for this claim. If multiple classes match the labels one will be chosen at random.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**matchExpressions**|[[DatabaseCrossplaneIoV1alpha1PostgreSQLInstanceSpecClassSelectorMatchExpressionsItems0](#databasecrossplaneiov1alpha1postgresqlinstancespecclassselectormatchexpressionsitems0)]|matchExpressions is a list of label selector requirements. The requirements are ANDed.||
|**matchLabels**|{str:str}|matchLabels is a map of {key,value} pairs. A single {key,value} in the matchLabels map is equivalent to an element of matchExpressions, whose key field is "key", the operator is "In", and the values array contains only "value". The requirements are ANDed.||
### DatabaseCrossplaneIoV1alpha1PostgreSQLInstanceSpecClassSelectorMatchExpressionsItems0

A label selector requirement is a selector that contains values, a key, and an operator that relates the key and values.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**key** `required`|str|key is the label key that the selector applies to.||
|**operator** `required`|str|operator represents a key's relationship to a set of values. Valid operators are In, NotIn, Exists and DoesNotExist.||
|**values**|[str]|values is an array of string values. If the operator is In or NotIn, the values array must be non-empty. If the operator is Exists or DoesNotExist, the values array must be empty. This array is replaced during a strategic merge patch.||
### DatabaseCrossplaneIoV1alpha1PostgreSQLInstanceSpecResourceRef

This syntax is chosen only to have some well-defined way of referencing a part of an object. TODO: this design is not final and this field is subject to change in the future.||
|**kind**|str|Kind of the referent. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#types-kinds||

### StorageCrossplaneIoV1alpha1BucketSpecClassRef

A ClassReference specifies a resource class that will be used to dynamically provision a managed resource when the resource claim is created.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**apiVersion**|str|API version of the referent.||
|**fieldPath**|str|If referring to a piece of an object instead of an entire object, this string should contain a valid JSON/Go field access statement, such as desiredState.manifest.containers[2]. For example, if the object reference is to a container within a pod, this would take on a value like: "spec.containers{name}" (where "name" refers to the name of the container that triggered the event) or if no container name is specified "spec.containers[2]" (container with index 2 in this pod). This syntax is chosen only to have some well-defined way of referencing a part of an object. TODO: this design is not final and this field is subject to change in the future.||
|**kind**|str|Kind of the referent. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#types-kinds||
|**name**|str|Name of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#names||
|**namespace**|str|Namespace of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/namespaces/||
|**resourceVersion**|str|Specific resourceVersion to which this reference is made, if any. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#concurrency-control-and-consistency||
|**uid**|str|UID of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#uids||
### StorageCrossplaneIoV1alpha1BucketSpecClassSelector

A ClassSelector specifies labels that will be used to select a resource class for this claim. If multiple classes match the labels one will be chosen at random.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**matchExpressions**|[[StorageCrossplaneIoV1alpha1BucketSpecClassSelectorMatchExpressionsItems0](#storagecrossplaneiov1alpha1bucketspecclassselectormatchexpressionsitems0)]|matchExpressions is a list of label selector requirements. The requirements are ANDed.||
|**matchLabels**|{str:str}|matchLabels is a map of {key,value} pairs. A single {key,value} in the matchLabels map is equivalent to an element of matchExpressions, whose key field is "key", the operator is "In", and the values array contains only "value". The requirements are ANDed.||
### StorageCrossplaneIoV1alpha1BucketSpecClassSelectorMatchExpressionsItems0

A label selector requirement is a selector that contains values, a key, and an operator that relates the key and values.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|**key** `required`|str|key is the label key that the selector applies to.||
|**operator** `required`|str|operator represents a key's relationship to a set of values. Valid operators are In, NotIn, Exists and DoesNotExist.||
|**values**|[str]|values is an array of string values. If the operator is In or NotIn, the values array must be non-empty. If the operator is Exists or DoesNotExist, the values array must be empty. This array is replaced during a strategic merge patch.||
### StorageCrossplaneIoV1alpha1BucketSpecResourceRef

A ResourceReference specifies an existing managed resource, in any namespace, to which this resource claim should attempt to bind. Omit the resource reference to enable dynamic provisioning using a resource class; the resource reference will be automatically populated by Crossplane.

#### Attributes

| name | type | description | default value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

For example, if the object reference is to a container within a pod, this would take on a value like: "spec.containers{name}" (where "name" refers to the name of the container that triggered the event) or if no container name is specified "spec.containers[2]" (container with index 2 in this pod). This syntax is chosen only to have some well-defined way of referencing a part of an object. TODO: this design is not final and this field is subject to change in the future.||
|**kind**|str|Kind of the referent. More info: https://git.k8s.io/community/contributors/devel/sig-architecture/api-conventions.md#types-kinds||
|**name**|str|Name of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/names/#names||
|**namespace**|str|Namespace of the referent. More info: https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/overview/working-with-objects/namespaces/||

### WorkloadCrossplaneIoV1alpha1KubernetesApplicationSpecResourceSelector

### ScopeDefinition

A ScopeDefinition registers a kind of Kubernetes custom resource as a valid OAM scope kind by referencing its CustomResourceDefinition. The CRD is used to validate the schema of the scope when it is embedded in an OAM ApplicationConfiguration.

### WorkloadDefinition

A WorkloadDefinition registers a kind of Kubernetes custom resource as a valid OAM workload kind by referencing its CustomResourceDefinition. The CRD is used to validate the schema of the workload when it is embedded in an OAM Component.
